### [302] [Sampling from Flow Language Models via Marginal-Conditioned Bridges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13681)
*Iskander Azangulov,Leo Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Flow Language Models (FLMs) use continuous flow matching for one-hot token sequences, with denoisers that model posterior marginals per token position. Standard DDPM samplers fail by collapsing these marginals into invalid one-hot endpoints. This paper proposes a training-free, posterior-predictive sampler: at each reverse step, it samples a clean one-hot token sequence from the FLM's marginal posteriors and then draws the intermediate state via an analytic Ornstein--Uhlenbeck bridge conditioned on this endpoint. The method preserves token-wise marginals, supports decoding controls (e.g., temperature, nucleus), and reduces approximation error—defined as conditional multi-information among positions. Theoretical analysis shows that the proposed bridge has lower denoising error than standard methods when intermediate observations provide additional information. Experiments confirm improved quality-diversity tradeoff in FLMs.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard DDPM-style samplers for Flow Language Models (FLMs) collapse posterior marginals into a single conditional-mean endpoint, which is typically not a valid one-hot sequence. This leads to suboptimal sampling quality and fails to leverage the full structure of FLMs. The motivation is to develop a principled, training-free sampling method that respects the factorized posterior structure of FLMs and enables better control over token-level generation.

Method: Proposes a posterior-predictive sampling framework for FLMs: 1) At each reverse step, sample a clean one-hot token sequence from the FLM’s learned marginal posteriors; 2) Use an analytic Ornstein--Uhlenbeck bridge to generate the intermediate continuous state conditioned on this sampled endpoint. The method requires no additional training, uses the same number of model evaluations as standard sampling, and supports standard decoding techniques like temperature scaling and nucleus truncation.

Result: The proposed sampler achieves a lower endpoint approximation error compared to standard DDPM-style methods, with the error bounded by the conditional multi-information across token positions. It preserves all token-wise posterior-predictive marginals and only loses residual cross-position dependencies. Girsanov path-space analysis proves that the marginal-conditioned bridge has no larger denoising error than the frozen conditional-mean bridge, with strict improvement when intermediate observations reveal additional information about the clean tokens. Empirical results show superior quality–diversity tradeoff in FLMs.

Conclusion: Posterior-predictive sampling is a principled and effective alternative to standard DDPM-style samplers for Flow Language Models. It fully leverages the structural properties of FLMs, improves generation quality and diversity, enables fine-grained decoding control, and comes with strong theoretical guarantees. The method is simple, training-free, and compatible with existing inference pipelines.

Abstract: Flow Language Models (FLMs) are a recently introduced class of language models which adapt continuous flow matching for one-hot encoded token sequences. Their denoisers have a special structure absent from generic continuous diffusion models: each block of the denoising mean is a posterior marginal distribution over the clean token at that position. Standard DDPM-style samplers collapse these marginals to a single conditional-mean endpoint and bridge toward this simplex-valued point, which is generally not a valid one-hot sequence. We argue that the natural sampler for an FLM is instead posterior-predictive. At each reverse step, we sample a clean one-hot endpoint from the factorized posterior defined by the FLM token marginals, and then sample the next continuous state from the analytic Ornstein--Uhlenbeck bridge conditioned on that endpoint. The method is training-free, uses the same model evaluations as standard sampling, and gives a principled interface for token-level decoding controls such as temperature scaling and nucleus truncation. We show that, under exact posterior marginals, the endpoint approximation error is exactly the conditional multi-information among token positions. The induced one-step bridge kernel preserves all token-wise posterior-predictive marginals and loses only the residual cross-position dependence. Finally, we prove a Girsanov path-space comparison showing that the marginal-conditioned bridge has a no-larger denoising-error term than the frozen conditional-mean bridge, with strict improvement whenever intermediate coordinate-wise bridge observations reveal additional information about the clean token. Experiments with FLMs show that the sampler improves the quality--diversity tradeoff. Code is available at: github.com/imbirik/mcb.

</details>


### [303] [Scale-Sensitive Shattering: Learnability and Evaluability at Optimal Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13684)
*Shashaank Aiyer,Yishay Mansour,Shay Moran,Han Shao,Tom Waknine*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究实值函数类在何种尺度下表现出一致收敛性和可学习性。核心结果建立了一个尺度敏感的PAC学习基本定理的推广：对于每个有界实值函数类和任意 $\gamma>0$，在尺度 $\gamma$ 下的一致收敛、在尺度 $\gamma/2$ 下的广义可学习性，以及在所有尺度 $\gamma'>\gamma$ 下的fat-shattering维数有限性三者等价。该结果解决了Anthony和Bartlett（1999）提出的关于学习性决定尺度的精确问题，推翻了Phil Long提出的‘2倍因子间隙不可避免’的猜想，并改进了Bartlett与Long（1998）的上界，避免了此类损失。关键技术在于直接对经验 $\ell_\infty$ 覆盖数进行估计，避免了传统通过填充数的迂回路径。由此得到关于fat-shattering尺度 $\gamma$ 的渐近度量熵的紧界：在尺度 $\gamma/2$ 下为 $O(\log^2 n)$，在尺度 $2\gamma$ 下为 $O(\log n)$，且 $O(\log^2 n)$ 界有时是紧的。这些结果解决了Alon等人（1997）和Rudelson-Vershynin（2006）的开放问题。作为应用，建立了有界积分概率度量的尖锐二分性：每个此类IPM要么可估计，要么无法在任何乘性因子 $c<3$ 内弱评估，而 $3$-弱评估总是成立，解决了Aiyer等人（ICML 2026）的开放问题。同时指出了若干关于样本复杂度和可评估性的开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究实值函数类在不同尺度下的统一收敛性与可学习性之间的关系，旨在精确刻画决定学习能力的尺度参数。此前存在关于是否必须存在2倍因子差距的争议，且已有上界存在损失，因此亟需更精细的分析框架。

Method: 提出一种直接估计经验 $\ell_\infty$ 覆盖数的方法，绕开传统的基于填充数的分析路径；结合fat-shattering维度的尺度特性，建立一致性收敛、可学习性与维度有限性之间的等价关系。

Result: 证明了在尺度 $\gamma$ 下一致收敛、尺度 $\gamma/2$ 下广义可学习性、以及所有 $\gamma'>\gamma$ 下fat-shattering维数有限性三者等价；给出了 $O(\log^2 n)$ 和 $O(\log n)$ 的紧度量熵界，并指出前者有时是紧的；揭示了积分概率度量的 $3$-弱评估的尖锐界限。

Conclusion: 本工作提供了对实值函数类学习性尺度的完整刻画，解决了多个长期存在的开放问题，推动了统计学习理论中关于样本复杂度和可评估性的理解，为后续研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We study the optimal scale at which real-valued function classes exhibit uniform convergence and learnability. Our main result establishes a scale-sensitive generalization of the fundamental theorem of PAC learning: for every bounded real-valued class and every $γ>0$, uniform convergence at scale $γ$, agnostic learnability at scale $γ/2$, and finiteness of the fat-shattering dimension at every scale $γ'>γ$ are equivalent. This resolves a question by Anthony and Bartlett (Cambridge Univ. Press 1999) on the precise scales governing learnability, refuting a conjecture attributed there to Phil Long that a multiplicative 2-factor gap is unavoidable, and improves the upper bounds of Bartlett and Long (JCSS 1998), which incur such a loss.
  The key technical ingredient is a direct bound on empirical $\ell_\infty$ covering numbers, avoiding the standard detour through packing numbers. As a consequence, we obtain sharp asymptotic metric-entropy bounds in terms of the fat-shattering scale $γ$: an $O(\log^2 n)$ bound holds already at scale $γ/2$, while an $O(\log n)$ bound holds at scale $2γ$. We further show that the $O(\log^2 n)$ bound is sometimes tight. These results resolve open questions by Alon et al. (JACM 1997) and Rudelson and Vershynin (Ann. of Math. 2006).
  As an application, we establish a sharp dichotomy for bounded integral probability metrics: every such IPM is either estimable or cannot be weakly evaluated within any multiplicative factor $c<3$, while $3$-weak evaluability always holds, resolving an open question from Aiyer et al. (ICML 2026). We also highlight several open questions on quantitative sample complexity and evaluability.

</details>


### [304] [A Hierarchical Language Model with Predictable Scaling Laws and Provable Benefits of Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13687)

Abstract: We introduce a family of synthetic languages with hierarchical structure -- generated by a broadcast process on trees -- for which the role of context length and reasoning in autoregressive generation can be analyzed precisely. At the heart of our analytic approach is an \emph{exact $k$-gram ansatz} in place of transformers with context length $k$, a substitution we then validate empirically. Using this ansatz we derive explicit asymptotic predictions for distributional statistics of the sequences produced by a trained model, instantiated in two settings. For the \emph{Ising broadcast process} (a soft-constrained language), we prove that the variance of the generated sum scales log-linearly in the context depth and its kurtosis converges to that of a Gaussian -- both deviating from the true language for any sublinear context. For the \emph{coloring broadcast process} (a hard-constrained language) in the freezing regime, bounded-context autoregression produces sequences that, with high probability, are inconsistent with \emph{any} valid coloring of the underlying tree. Together these results imply an $Ω(n)$ lower bound on the context length required to faithfully sample length-$n$ sequences. In contrast, we prove that an autoregressive \emph{reasoning} model with only $Θ(\log n)$ working memory can sample exactly from the true language -- an exponential improvement. We confirm both the lower-bound predictions and the reasoning-based upper bound empirically with transformers trained on the synthetic language; the trained models track our asymptotic predictions quantitatively across a wide range of context sizes.

### [305] [Polyhedral Instability Governs Regret in Online Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13692)
*Yuetai Li,Fengqing Jiang,Yichen Feng,Kaiyuan Zheng,Luyao Niu,Bhaskar Ramasubramanian,Basel Alomair,Linda Bushnell,Radha Poovendran*

TL;DR: 该论文研究了组合动作在线决策问题中的凸松弛方法，发现其后悔率由多面体不稳定性（即活跃区域变化次数）决定。在全信息反馈和固定划分假设下，后悔率与区域切换次数和每区域最大顶点数相关，介于专家类似和维度依赖的在线凸优化速率之间。对于洛瓦兹凸化下的在线子模-凹博弈，后悔率简化为排列切换次数，验证了理论预测的缩放行为，并表明在实际中无需显式枚举动作即可出现低不稳定性状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决在线组合决策问题中由于动作空间庞大导致的计算挑战，通过凸松弛方法将问题转化为在线凸优化，探究其后悔率的本质因素。

Method: 基于凸松弛的在线凸优化框架，分析多面体结构下的区域切换行为，引入多面体不稳定性概念，并在全信息反馈与固定划分假设下推导后悔率边界。

Result: 证明了后悔率与区域切换次数和每区域顶点数的平方根成正比，具体为 $\Regret_T= Θ(\sqrt{(1+\mathrm{RS}_T)\,T\,\log V_{\max}})$；在子模-凹博弈中，简化为 $\Regret_T= Θ(\sqrt{(1+\mathrm{SC}_T)\,T\,\log n})$，实验验证了理论预测。

Conclusion: 多面体不稳定性是控制在线组合优化后悔率的关键因素，理论结果与实验一致，表明在实际问题中可实现低不稳定性，从而提升算法性能。

Abstract: Many online decision problems over combinatorial actions are addressed via convex relaxations, leading to online convex optimization with piecewise linear objectives and induced polyhedral structure. We show that regret in such problems is governed by \emph{polyhedral instability}: the number of changes of the active region. Under full information feedback and fixed partition assumptions, if $\mathrm{RS}_T$ denotes the number of region switches and $V_{\max}$ the maximum number of vertices per region, we prove $\Regret_T= Θ(\sqrt{(1+\mathrm{RS}_T)\,T\,\log V_{\max}})$ interpolating between experts-like and dimension-dependent OCO rates. For online submodular--concave games under Lovász convexification, this reduces to the permutation-switch count $\mathrm{SC}_T$, yielding the matching rate $\Regret_T= Θ(\sqrt{(1+\mathrm{SC}_T)\,T\,\log n})$. Experiments on synthetic and real combinatorial problems (shortest path, influence maximization) validate the predicted scaling and indicate that low-instability regimes can arise in practice without explicit enumeration of actions.

### [306] [MILM: Large Language Models for Multimodal Irregular Time Series with Informative Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13711)
*Hsing-Huan Chung,Shijun Li,Yoav Wald,Xing Han,Suchi Saria,Joydeep Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MILM 是一种用于处理多模态不规则时间序列（MITS）的模型，将异步、不规则采样的数值与文本数据表示为时间有序的XML三元组，并通过两阶段微调策略训练LLM进行分类。第一阶段仅基于采样模式预测，第二阶段联合建模采样模式与观测值。实验表明，MILM-2S在多个电子健康记录（EHR）数据集上表现最佳，且采样模式本身具有预测价值。在部分值缺失场景下，MILM-2S显著优于单阶段模型，且保留缺失值的时间与通道信息可进一步提升院内死亡率预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态不规则时间序列（MITS）在医疗等场景中普遍存在，其异步采样模式和通道多样性蕴含重要预测信号，但传统方法难以有效融合数值与文本特征。大语言模型（LLM）具备跨模态理解能力，但如何利用其处理不规则时间序列仍具挑战。因此，亟需一种能有效建模采样模式与内容信息的框架。

Method: 将MITS表示为时间有序的XML三元组；提出两阶段微调策略：第一阶段使用去值化数据训练以学习采样模式；第二阶段使用完整数据联合建模采样模式与观测值；引入单阶段对比模型（MILM-Direct）进行性能比较。

Result: MILM-2S在多个EHR数据集上取得最佳平均性能，优于现有方法；消融实验验证采样模式具有显著预测能力；在值缺失场景下，MILM-2S相比MILM-Direct优势更大；保留缺失值的时间与通道信息可进一步提升预测效果。

Conclusion: MILM通过两阶段策略有效捕捉了多模态不规则时间序列中的采样模式与内容信息，在真实医疗场景中表现出强鲁棒性与优越性能，尤其在值缺失情况下更具优势，证明采样模式是重要的预测线索。

Abstract: Multimodal irregular time series (MITS) consist of asynchronous and irregularly sampled observations from heterogeneous numerical and textual channels. In healthcare, for example, patients' electronic health records (EHR) include irregular lab measurements and clinical notes. The irregular timing and channel patterns of observations carry predictive signal alongside the numerical values and textual content. LLMs are natural candidates for processing such heterogeneous data, given their extensive pretrained knowledge spanning textual and numerical domains. We introduce MILM (Multimodal Irregular time series Language Model), which represents MITS as time-ordered triplets in Extensible Markup Language (XML) format and fine-tunes an LLM through a two-stage strategy for MITS classification. The first stage trains on value-redacted MITS to predict from sampling patterns alone, and the second stage trains on full MITS to jointly model sampling patterns and observed values. Our two-stage model (MILM-2S) and its single-stage counterpart (MILM-Direct) achieve the best and second-best average performance on multiple EHR datasets. Further value redaction evaluations confirm that sampling patterns carry predictive signal and that MILM-2S learns to exploit them. In the value pending evaluation we introduce, where some values are unavailable at prediction time, MILM-2S outperforms MILM-Direct by a larger margin compared to standard evaluation. For MILM-2S, preserving the time and channel of value-pending observations as additional sampling information further improves in-hospital mortality prediction.

</details>


### [307] [Tight Sample Complexity Bounds for Entropic Best Policy Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13717)
*Amer Essakine,Claire Vernade*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究有限时域风险敏感强化学习中基于熵风险度量的最佳策略识别问题。针对已有工作在样本复杂度上下界之间存在指数级差距的问题，本文通过引入基于前向模型的算法，并结合KL-探索奖励机制，提出两项关键技术改进：利用指数效用函数的光滑性获得更紧的集中界，设计新的停止规则以充分利用这种紧致性，最终实现了与下界匹配的样本复杂度，从而填补了该领域的理论空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究在有限时域风险敏感强化学习中，最佳策略识别的样本复杂度上下界之间存在指数级差距，上界为 $O(e^{2|β| H})$，而下界为 $Ω(e^{|β| H})$，这一差距源于对指数效用的集中控制过于宽松。因此，亟需更精细的分析方法来缩小甚至消除该差距。

Method: 提出一种基于前向模型的算法，采用KL-based探索奖励机制，并针对熵风险准则进行适配；通过利用指数效用函数的光滑性，推导出更紧的集中不等式；设计新的停止规则以进一步利用集中性的提升，从而降低样本复杂度。

Result: 所提算法实现了与已知下界一致的样本复杂度，即 $O(e^{|β| H})$，首次在理论上完全匹配下界，解决了该问题中的开放性难题。

Conclusion: 通过引入更精细的集中分析和优化的停止规则，本文成功将风险敏感强化学习中最佳策略识别的样本复杂度从 $O(e^{2|β| H})$ 降低至与下界一致的 $O(e^{|β| H})$，显著推进了该领域的理论进展。

Abstract: We study best-policy identification for finite-horizon risk-sensitive reinforcement learning under the entropic risk measure. Recent work established a constant gap in the exponential horizon dependence between lower and upper bounds on the number of samples required to identify an approximately optimal policy. Precisely, known lower bounds scale in $Ω(e^{|β| H})$ where $H$ is the horizon of the MDP, while the state-of-the-art upper bound achieves at best $O(e^{2|β| H})$ (arXiv:2506.00286v2) using a generative model. We show that this extra exponential factor can be traced to overly loose concentration control for exponential utilities. To close this open gap, we revisit the analysis of this problem through a forward-model based algorithm building on KL-based exploration bonuses that we adapt to the entropic criterion. The improvement we get is due to two main novel technical innovations. We leverage the smoothness properties of the exponential utility to derive sharper concentration bounds, and we propose a new stopping rule that exploits further this tightness to obtain a sample complexity that matches the lower bound.

### [309] [Learning POMDP World Models from Observations with Language-Model Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13740)
*Valentin Six,Frederik Panse,Mathis Fajeau,Lancelot Da Costa,Mridul Sharma,Alfonso Amayuelas,Tim Z. Xiao,David Hyland,Philipp Hennig,Bernhard Schölkopf*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Pinductor利用语言模型先验，从少量观测-动作轨迹中提出候选的POMDP模型，并通过迭代优化信念似然得分来改进模型。尽管信息量较少，其性能和样本效率可媲美依赖隐藏状态信息的LLM方法，显著优于传统表格型POMDP基线。性能随LLM能力提升而增强，且在缺乏语义信息时表现平稳下降，表明语言模型先验能有效促进部分可观测环境下的世界模型学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在部分可观测环境中，传统POMDP学习需要大量环境交互，成本高昂。本文旨在探索是否可通过语言模型先验，利用已有知识减少对环境交互的依赖，实现更高效的内部世界模型学习。

Method: 提出Pinductor框架：基于大型语言模型（LLM）从少量观察-动作轨迹中生成候选POMDP模型，并通过迭代优化信念相关的似然分数进行精炼，从而在不依赖隐藏状态的前提下构建准确的世界模型。

Result: Pinductor在仅使用有限信息的情况下，达到与依赖隐藏状态的先进方法相当的性能和样本效率，显著超越传统表格型POMDP方法；其性能随语言模型能力提升而上升，且在语义信息缺失时表现平稳退化，验证了语言模型先验的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 语言模型先验可作为高效世界模型学习的重要工具，尤其适用于部分可观测场景，有助于推动通用智能体在真实世界中的应用。代码已开源。

Abstract: Whether navigating a building, operating a robot, or playing a game, an agent that acts effectively in an environment must first learn an internal model of how that environment works. Partially-observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs) provide a flexible modeling class for such internal world models, but learning them from observation-action trajectories alone is challenging and typically requires extensive environment interaction. We ask whether language-model priors can reduce costly interaction by leveraging prior knowledge, and introduce \emph{Pinductor} (POMDP-inductor): an LLM proposes candidate POMDP models from a few observation-action trajectories and iteratively refines them to optimize a belief-based likelihood score. Despite using strictly less information, \emph{Pinductor} matches the performance and sample efficiency of LLM-based POMDP learning methods that assume privileged access to the hidden state, while significantly surpassing the sample efficiency of tabular POMDP baselines. Further results show that performance scales with LLM capability and degrades gracefully as semantic information about the environment is withheld. Together, these results position language-model priors as a practical tool for sample-efficient world-model learning under partial observability, and a step toward generalist agents in real-world environments. Code is available at https://github.com/atomresearch/pinductor.

Result: （i）建筑级排放预测结构上比公司级更困难；（ii）分布外迁移误差远大于模型间差异，且表格式基础模型首次在多城市建筑排放任务中显著优于调优的树模型；（iii）遥感多模态嵌入在表格模型泛化失败处提供了关键帮助。同时识别出城市间灾难性迁移和行业因子查找的性能天花板等系统性失败模式。

Abstract: Open datasets and benchmarks for entity-level carbon-emission prediction remain fragmented across access, scale, granularity, and evaluation. We introduce GHGbench, an open dataset and benchmark for company- and building-level greenhouse-gas prediction. The company track contains 32,000+ company-year records from 12,000+ firms with Scope 1+2 and Scope 3 disclosures and financial/sectoral signals; the building track harmonises 491,591 building-year records from 13 open sources into a single schema across 26 metropolitan areas (10 U.S., 15 Australian, 1 Singaporean), with climate covariates and multimodal remote-sensing embeddings. GHGbench defines canonical splits with in-distribution and cross-region/city transfer as primary tasks and temporal hold-out plus short-horizon forecasting as supplementary appendix evidence; headline baselines span gradient-boosted trees, a tabular foundation model, MLP, FT-Transformer, and multimodal fusion, with an LLM panel as auxiliary, all evaluated under multi-seed paired-bootstrap tests. Three benchmark-level findings emerge: (i) building emissions are structurally harder than company emissions; (ii) the in-distribution to out-of-distribution gap dwarfs any within-model gap across both the company track and the building track, and a tabular foundation model is, to our knowledge, the first baseline to open a paired-bootstrap-significant gap over tuned trees on a multi-city building-emissions task; (iii) multimodal remote-sensing embeddings help precisely where tabular generalisation breaks. GHGbench also exposes catastrophic city transfer and the sector-factor lookup ceiling as systematic failure modes. Code and reconstruction recipes are available at GHGbench.

Method: 提出一个通用的公平聚类框架，基于该框架设计三种启发式算法：1）高精度与灵活约束支持；2）高效可扩展且保持高质量；3）极致可扩展，适用于大规模数据。通过优化目标函数和引入公平性约束，实现对成本与公平性的精细调控。

Abstract: Clustering is an unsupervised machine learning task that consists of identifying groups of similar objects. It has numerous applications and is increasingly used in fairness-sensitive domains where objects represent individuals, such as customers, employees, or students. We address a fair clustering problem in which objects belong to protected groups. The problem consists of partitioning the objects into a predefined number of clusters while attaining a user-defined target level of fairness, meaning that each protected group is sufficiently represented in each cluster. The objective is to minimize the clustering cost, defined as the sum of squared Euclidean distances between the objects and the centers of their clusters. Since clustering cost and fairness are generally in conflict, managing the trade-off between them is essential in practical applications. Existing methods provide limited control over this trade-off and either fail to scale to large datasets or, when they scale, produce low-quality solutions. We propose a general framework for fair clustering that provides precise control over the cost-fairness trade-off and introduce three heuristics based on it. The first heuristic focuses on solution quality and the flexibility to incorporate additional constraints, the second improves scalability while retaining high solution quality, and the third is designed for maximum scalability, producing solutions for instances with millions of objects in seconds. The proposed heuristics outperform existing approaches in comprehensive numerical experiments on benchmark datasets. The source code of our heuristics and instructions for reproducing the experiments are publicly available on GitHub.

### [312] [High-Rate Quantized Matrix Multiplication II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13768)
*Or Ordentlich,Yury Polyanskiy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在已知协方差矩阵 $Σ_X$ 条件下的量化矩阵乘法（MatMul），适用于大模型权重仅量化（weight-only post-training quantization）场景。通过引入经典水填（waterfilling）理论优化率分配，提出改进的GPTQ算法，并分析了WaterSIC方案的高率性能：其性能与基底无关，且距离信息论极限仅差约0.25 bit/entry。实验表明，使用随机旋转的GPTQ在高率下也接近最优，误差小于0.1 bit/entry。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量化方法如GPTQ在率分配上采用均匀方式，未考虑数据协方差结构；而实际中权重分布具有结构性特征，尤其在大模型量化中，利用协方差信息可提升压缩效率。因此需要设计更优的率分配策略以逼近信息论极限。

Method: 基于加权均方误差（WMSE）源编码框架，引入水填（waterfilling）原理进行最优率分配；分析并改进GPTQ算法，结合实际大模型（Llama-3-8B）的协方差矩阵 $Σ_X$ 进行性能评估；对比WaterSIC与GPTQ在不同基底和层类型下的表现。

Result: WaterSIC在高率下性能与基底无关，且距离信息论极限仅差0.25 bit/entry；GPTQ在随机旋转下性能接近WaterSIC，误差低于0.1 bit/entry，表明其在高率下已接近最优。

Conclusion: 通过引入水填原理优化率分配，显著提升了权重仅量化算法的性能。即使不依赖特定基底，WaterSIC仍能实现近似最优压缩；而当前主流的GPTQ在随机旋转下亦表现出极佳性能，说明其在高率场景下具备良好的适应性与接近最优的能力。

Abstract: This is the second part of the work investigating quantized matrix multiplication (MatMul). In part I we considered the case of calibration-free quantization, whereas here we discuss the setting where covariance matrix $Σ_X$ of the columns of the second factor is available. This setting arises in the ubiquitous task of weight-only post-training quantization of LLMs.
  Weight-only quantization is related to the problem of weighted mean squared error (WMSE) source coding, whose classical (reverse) waterfilling solution dictates how one should distribute rate between coordinates of the vector. We show how waterfilling can be used to improve practical LLM quantization algorithms (GPTQ), which at present allocate rate equally. A recent scheme (known as ``WaterSIC'') that only uses scalar INT quantizers is analyzed and its high-rate performance is shown to be (a) basis free (i.e., characterized by the determinant of $Σ_X$ and, thus, unlike existing schemes, is immune to applying random rotations); and (b) within a multiplicative factor of $\frac{2πe}{12}$ (or 0.25 bit/entry) of the information-theoretic distortion limit. GPTQ's performance, in turn, is affected by the choice of basis, but for a random rotation and actual $Σ_X$ from Llama-3-8B we find it to be within 0.1 bit (depending on the layer type) of WaterSIC, suggesting that GPTQ with random rotation is also near optimal, at least in the high-rate regime.

### [313] [MinT: Managed Infrastructure for Training and Serving Millions of LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13779)
*Mind Lab,:,Song Cao,Vic Cao,Andrew Chen,Kaijie Chen,Cleon Cheng,Steven Chiang,Kaixuan Fan,Hera Feng,Huan Feng,Arthur Fu,Jun Gao,Hongquan Gu,Aaron Guan,Nolan Ho,Mutian Hong,Hailee Hou,Peixuan Hua,Charles Huang,Miles Jiang,Nora Jiang,Yuyi Jiang,Qiuyu Jin,Fancy Kong,Andrew Lei,Kyrie Lei,Alexy Li,Lucian Li,Ray Li,Theo Li,Zhihui Li,Jiayi Lin,Kairus Liu,Kieran Liu,Logan Liu,Xiang Liu,Irvine Lu,Maeve Luo,Runze Lv,Pony Ma,Verity Niu,Anson Qiu,Vincent Wang,Rio Yang,Maxwell Yao,Carrie Ye,Regis Ye,Wenlin Ye,Josh Ying,Danney Zeng,Yuhan Zhan,Anya Zhang,Di Zhang,Ruijia Zhang,Sueky Zhang,Ya Zhang,Wei Zhao,Ada Zhou,Changhai Zhou,Yuhua Zhou,Xinyue Zhu,Murphy Zhuang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MinT 是一个用于低秩适应（LoRA）后训练和在线服务的托管基础设施系统，支持大规模策略管理。它通过保持基础模型驻留、仅传输轻量级 LoRA 适配器，实现了在扩展性、效率和资源利用率上的三重提升：Scale Up 支持超大规模密集模型与 MoE 架构的训练与服务；Scale Down 实现适配器体积小于基础模型 1%，显著降低传输开销；Scale Out 将策略可寻址性与计算资源分离，支持百万级策略目录和千级活跃适配器并行处理。整体实现千万级策略管理，共享 1T 级基础模型进行高效训练与服务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在多策略生成与部署场景中面临高昂存储成本、高传输开销和资源调度复杂性问题。尤其当基础模型庞大时，频繁合并完整检查点不可持续，亟需一种高效、可扩展的管理机制来支持大量策略的快速迭代与在线服务。

Method: MinT 采用基础模型常驻、仅传输 LoRA 适配器的架构，结合分布式训练与服务调度，通过三轴扩展策略实现高效管理：（1）Scale Up 引入 MLA/DSA 注意力路径，支持万亿参数级模型训练与服务；（2）Scale Down 仅传输小尺寸适配器，减少数据移动开销；（3）Scale Out 实现策略地址空间与计算工作集解耦，利用张量并行与打包 MoE LoRA 提升加载效率。所有流程通过统一服务接口抽象，隐藏底层复杂性。

Result: MinT 成功在 4B 密集模型上将传输步骤减少 18.3 倍，在 30B MoE 模型上减少 2.85 倍；并发多策略训练使墙时缩短 1.77 倍和 1.45 倍，且峰值内存未增加；单引擎支持 10 万次策略扫描，集群规模下可管理百万级策略目录，活加载速度提升 8.5–8.7 倍。系统验证了在共享 1T 级基础模型上对千万级策略的高效管理能力。

Conclusion: MinT 为大规模低秩适应策略的后训练与在线服务提供了一套高效、可扩展的基础设施解决方案，显著降低了存储与通信开销，提升了资源利用率与部署效率，是实现低成本、高并发策略迭代的关键技术。

Abstract: We present MindLab Toolkit (MinT), a managed infrastructure system for Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) post-training and online serving. MinT targets a setting where many trained policies are produced over a small number of expensive base-model deployments. Instead of materializing each policy as a merged full checkpoint, MinT keeps the base model resident and moves exported LoRA adapter revisions through rollout, update, export, evaluation, serving, and rollback, hiding distributed training, serving, scheduling, and data movement behind a service interface. MinT scales this path along three axes. Scale Up extends LoRA RL to frontier-scale dense and MoE architectures, including MLA and DSA attention paths, with training and serving validated beyond 1T total parameters. Scale Down moves only the exported LoRA adapter, which can be under 1% of base-model size in rank-1 settings; adapter-only handoff reduces the measured step by 18.3x on a 4B dense model and 2.85x on a 30B MoE, while concurrent multi-policy GRPO shortens wall time by 1.77x and 1.45x without raising peak memory. Scale Out separates durable policy addressability from CPU/GPU working sets: a tensor-parallel deployment supports 10^6-scale addressable catalogs (measured single-engine sweeps through 100K) and thousand-adapter active waves at cluster scale, with cold loading treated as scheduled service work and packed MoE LoRA tensors improving live engine loading by 8.5-8.7x. MinT thus manages million-scale LoRA policy catalogs while training and serving selected adapter revisions over shared 1T-class base models.

</details>


### [314] [Attention Once Is All You Need: Efficient Streaming Inference with Stateful Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13784)
*Victor Norgren*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种以状态会话为中心的数据驱动计算模型，通过增量更新持久化的键值缓存，将预填充成本移出关键路径，使查询延迟与累积上下文大小无关。Flash Queries 利用数据到达间隙的空闲 GPU 周期提前评估注册问题并返回缓存答案，显著提升效率。结合多租户连续批处理调度器，可在单个 GPU 上支持数十个状态会话，同时保持完整的二次自注意力能力。在流式市场数据基准测试中，相比传统推理引擎（vLLM、SGLang、TensorRT-LLM、llama.cpp），参考实现达到最高 5.9 倍加速，且查询延迟不随上下文增长而增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统 Transformer 推理引擎为请求驱动，每次查询需支付 O(n) 的预填充开销，在持续流式工作负载中，随着上下文不断增长，该开销变得不可接受。需要一种能有效处理长上下文流式数据的新范式。

Method: 引入基于状态会话的数据驱动计算模型，使用持续更新的键值缓存避免重复预填充；利用空闲 GPU 周期进行前置查询评估（Flash Queries）；设计多租户连续批处理调度器，支持按单元预算准入和前缀感知的分组预填充。

Result: 在流式市场数据基准上，参考实现相较 vLLM、SGLang、TensorRT-LLM、llama.cpp 等传统引擎最高提速 5.9 倍，同时保持查询延迟恒定，不受累积上下文长度影响。

Conclusion: 所提出的架构实现了高效、低延迟的流式推理，突破了传统请求驱动模型在长上下文场景下的性能瓶颈，为大规模实时推理提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Conventional transformer inference engines are request-driven, paying an O(n) prefill cost on every query. In streaming workloads, where data arrives continuously and queries probe an ever-growing context, this cost is prohibitive. We introduce a data-driven computational model centred on stateful sessions: a persistent KV cache advanced incrementally as new data arrives, so prefill is moved off the critical path and query latency becomes O(|q|), independent of accumulated context size. Building on this, Flash Queries reclaim idle GPU cycles between data arrivals to pre-evaluate registered questions and return cached answers before the user asks, a pattern that is structurally impossible in stateless engines because they discard intermediate state between requests. A multi-tenant continuous-batching scheduler with cell-budget admission and prefix-aware grouped prefill lets dozens of stateful sessions coexist on a single GPU while preserving full quadratic self-attention. On streaming market-data benchmarks the reference implementation achieves up to 5.9x speedup over conventional inference engines (vLLM, SGLang, TensorRT-LLM, llama.cpp), holding query latency constant as accumulated context grows.

### [315] [Interpretable Machine Learning for Antepartum Prediction of Pregnancy-Associated Thrombotic Microangiopathy Using Routine Longitudinal Laboratory Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13786)
*Chuanchuan Sun,Zhen Yu,Qin Fan,Qingchao Chen,Feng Yu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 回顾性研究纳入300例妊娠，保留146个纵向实验室指标，采用分层抽样分为训练集（80%）和测试集（20%）。比较五种机器学习算法（逻辑回归、SVM、随机森林、极端随机树、梯度提升），基于交叉验证平均AUROC选择最优模型，最终在独立测试集上评估，并进行可解释性分析。

Abstract: Background: Pregnancy-associated thrombotic microangiopathy (P-TMA) is rare but life-threatening. Early risk prediction before overt clinical presentation remains challenging, as the associated laboratory abnormalities are subtle, multidimensional, and frequently masked by common physiological changes such as gestational thrombocytopenia and pregnancy-related proteinuria, thus overlapping heavily with benign obstetric and renal conditions. This complexity is poorly captured by univariate or rule-based approaches; however, it is addressable by machine learning, which can extract latent, time-dependent risk signatures from longitudinal clinical tests. Methods: This retrospective study included 300 pregnancies comprising 142 P-TMA cases and 158 controls. After exclusion of identifiers and non-informative variables, 146 longitudinal laboratory predictors were retained. Five algorithms were evaluated: logistic regression, support vector machine with radial basis function kernel, random forest, extra trees, and gradient boosting. The final model was selected by mean cross-validated AUROC, refitted on the full training cohort, and evaluated once in the held-out test cohort. Interpretability analyses examined global feature importance and distributional patterns of leading predictors. Results: Gradient boosting was prespecified by cross-validation in the training cohort. The model achieved an AUROC of 0.872 (95% CI: 0.769-0.952) and an AUPRC of 0.883 (95% CI: 0.780-0.959) in a held-out test cohort, with sensitivity of 0.750 and specificity of 0.812. Conclusions: Longitudinal clinical laboratory tests obtained during routine care contained informative and clinically plausible signals for P-TMA risk. ### [316] [Force-Aware Neural Tangent Kernels for Scalable and Robust Active Learning of MLIPs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13788)
*Eszter Varga-Umbrich,Zachary Weller-Davies,Paul Duckworth,Jules Tilly,Olivier Peltre,Shikha Surana*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可扩展的主动学习框架，用于机器学习原子间势（MLIPs），解决了大规模候选集筛选、能量-力联合监督和分布偏移鲁棒性等挑战。通过基于分块特征空间后验方差筛选的线性缩放方法，实现了对约20万结构的快速筛查。进一步将神经正切核（NTK）扩展至力感知设置，提出了力NTK与联合能量-力NTK，作为向量场预测的自然相似性度量。在OC20数据集上，该方法在所有指标和分布划分中均达到最低的能源和力误差；在T1x、PMechDB和RGD基准测试中，效率显著优于基于委员会的方法，且在受控偏移实验中表现出更强的鲁棒性。结果表明，单一预训练MLIP即可实现高效、力感知且分布鲁棒的主动学习，适用于基础模型微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出基于分块特征空间后验方差短选的线性缩放采集框架，避免计算候选集与训练集核矩阵，实现高效结构筛选；引入混合参数坐标导数，将神经正切核（NTK）推广至力感知场景，构建力NTK与联合能量-力NTK，作为向量场预测的相似性度量标准。

Result: 在OC20数据集上，所提力感知采集方法在能量和力的MAE与RMSE上均优于所有对比方法，表现最佳；在T1x、PMechDB和RGD等多个基准测试中，性能媲美主流基线，但计算效率显著更高；在候选池分布偏移的控制实验中，基于预训练模型嵌入与NTK的采集策略保持稳定，而委员会方法波动较大。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，通过结合预训练的机器学习原子间势与改进的力感知核方法，可实现可扩展、力敏感且对分布偏移具有鲁棒性的主动学习框架，为大规模材料模拟中的基础模型微调提供了高效可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Active learning for machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) must address several challenges to be practical: scaling to large candidate pools, leveraging energy-force supervision, and maintaining robustness when candidate pools are biased relative to the target distribution. In this work, we jointly address these challenges. We first introduce a linearly scaling acquisition framework based on chunked feature-space posterior-variance shortlisting. By avoiding materialisation of the candidate and train set kernels, this approach enables screening of ~200k structures within hours and applies broadly to acquisition strategies that score candidates based on molecular similarity metrics. We then extend the Neural Tangent Kernel (NTK) to a force-aware setting via mixed parameter-coordinate derivatives, yielding a force NTK and a joint energy-force NTK that provide natural similarity metrics for vector-field prediction. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the joint energy-force NTK on the OC20 dataset, where force-aware acquisition is crucial: it achieves the lowest energy and force MAE and RMSE across all metrics and distribution splits. Across T1x, PMechDB, and RGD benchmarks, our force NTK methods remain competitive with established baselines while being significantly more efficient than committee-based approaches. Under a controlled candidate-pool shift case study on T1x, acquisition based on pretrained MLIP embeddings and NTKs remains robust, whereas committee-based methods exhibit higher variance. Overall, these results show that a single pretrained MLIP can enable scalable, force-aware, and distribution-robust active learning for foundation-model fine-tuning.

### [317] [ENSEMBITS: an alphabet of protein conformational ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13789)
*Kaiwen Shi,Carlos Oliver*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Ensembits 是首个用于蛋白质构象集合的分词器，通过残差 VQ-VAE 与帧蒸馏目标在大规模分子动力学数据上训练，能够捕捉蛋白质动态特性，包括相关运动和不同构象状态。它在均方根漂移预测（RMSF）和残基运动幅度预测方面优于现有方法，并在酶分类（EC）、基因本体（GO）、结合位点/亲和力预测以及零样本突变效应预测任务中表现媲美甚至超越静态分词器，同时使用更少的预训练数据。其蒸馏机制还能从单一预测结构中推断出动态分词，缓解动态数据稀疏问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用残差 VQ-VAE 架构，结合帧蒸馏目标函数，在大规模分子动力学数据上训练；设计了对可变大小集合具有置换不变性的编码方式，并提取跨构象的有意义几何描述符以应对动态数据稀疏性挑战。

Result: Ensembits 在 RMSF 预测任务上表现最佳，在残基运动幅度的 ANOVA 测试中作为独立结构分词器最强；在多种下游任务（如 EC、GO、结合位点/亲和力预测、零样本突变效应预测）中达到或超过静态分词器性能，且所需预训练数据显著减少。此外，可通过单个结构预测动态分词，有效缓解动态数据稀缺问题。

Conclusion: 随着蛋白质研究从静态结构预测转向集合生成，Ensembits 提供了将动态信息融入蛋白质语言模型与设计的关键离散词汇工具，推动蛋白质语言建模进入动态时代。

Abstract: Protein structure tokenizers (PSTs) are workhorses in protein language modeling, function prediction, and evolutionary analysis. However, existing PSTs only capture local geometry of static structures, and miss the correlated motions and alternative conformational states revealed by protein ensembles. Here we introduce Ensembits, the first tokenizer of protein conformational ensembles. Ensembits address challenges inherent to tokenizing dynamics: deriving informative geometric descriptors across conformations, permutation-invariance encoding of variable-size ensembles, and conquering sparsity in dynamics data. Trained with a Residual VQ-VAE using a frame distillation objective on a large molecular dynamics corpus, Ensembits outperforms all related methods on RMSF prediction, and is the strongest standalone structural tokenizer on an token-conditioned ANOVA test on per-residue motion amplitude. Ensembits further matches or exceeds static tokenizers on EC, GO, binding site/affinity prediction, and zero-shot mutation-effect prediction despite using far less pretraining data. Notably, the distillation objective enables Ensembits to predict dynamics token from one single predicted structure, which alleviates dynamics data sparsity. As the field moves from static structure prediction toward ensemble generation, Ensembits offer the discrete vocabulary needed to bring dynamics into protein language modeling and design.

### [318] [Di-BiLPS: Denoising induced Bidirectional Latent-PDE-Solver under Sparse Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13790)
*Zhonghao Li,Chaoyu Liu,Qian Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Di-BiLPS 是一种统一的神经框架，用于在极稀疏观测下高效解决前向和反向偏微分方程（PDE）问题。通过变分自编码器压缩高维输入至紧凑潜在空间，结合潜在扩散模块建模不确定性，并利用对比学习对齐表示，实现高效推理与灵活映射。引入基于方差保持扩散过程的PDE感知去噪算法，进一步提升效率。实验表明，该方法在极端稀疏数据（低至3%）下表现优于现有方法，显著降低计算成本，并支持零样本超分辨率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经方法在极端稀疏观测下准确率下降且推理效率低，经典数值方法也受限于稀疏数据，亟需一种高效、鲁棒且适用于极稀疏场景的统一框架。

Method: 采用变分自编码器进行数据压缩，构建潜在空间；引入潜在扩散模块以建模不确定性；使用对比学习对齐特征表示；设计PDE感知的方差保持去噪算法以提升推理效率。所有操作均在潜在空间中完成，实现高效推理与灵活映射。

Result: 在多个PDE基准测试中，Di-BiLPS 在极稀疏输入（最低3%采样率）下持续达到最先进性能，显著降低计算开销，并具备零样本超分辨率能力，可预测连续时空域。

Conclusion: Di-BiLPS 为极稀疏观测下的前向与反向PDE问题提供了一个高效、准确且通用的解决方案，兼具推理效率与泛化能力，具有广泛应用潜力。

Abstract: Partial differential equations (PDEs) are fundamental for modeling complex natural and physical phenomena. In many real-world applications, however, observational data are extremely sparse, which severely limits the applicability of both classical numerical solvers and existing neural approaches. While neural methods have shown promising results under moderately sparse observations, their inference efficiency at high resolutions is limited, and their accuracy degrades substantially in the extremely sparse regime. In this work, we propose the Di-BiLPS, a unified neural framework that effectively handle both forward and inverse PDE problems under extremely sparse observations. Di-BiLPS combines a variational autoencoder to compress high-dimensional inputs into a compact latent space, a latent diffusion module to model uncertainty, and contrastive learning to align representations. Operating entirely in this latent space, the framework achieves efficient inference while retaining flexible input-output mapping. In addition, we introduce a PDE-informed denoising algorithm based on a variance-preserving diffusion process, which further improves inference efficiency. Extensive experiments on multiple PDE benchmarks demonstrate that Di-BiLPS consistently achieves SOTA performance under extremely sparse inputs (as low as 3%), while substantially reducing computational cost. Moreover, Di-BiLPS enables zero-shot super-resolution, as it allows predictions over continuous spatial-temporal domains.

### [320] [Provable Quantization with Randomized Hadamard Transform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13810)
*Ying Feng,Piotr Indyk,Michael Kapralov,Dmitry Krachun,Boris Prokhorov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种基于单个随机哈达玛变换的加抖动量化方法，通过在哈达玛变换后减去随机标量偏移来引入额外随机性，实现了与真实随机旋转矩阵相当的均方误差性能，且计算复杂度仅为O(d log d)。该方法在理论上证明了无偏性，并给出了渐近最优的压缩误差界，适用于相似性搜索、联邦学习和KV缓存压缩等场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于随机投影的向量量化方法中，密集随机旋转虽理论性能优越但计算开销大（Θ(d²)），而哈达玛变换虽降低了复杂度至O(d log d)，但其离散结构导致分析困难且压缩保证较弱。因此需要一种兼具高效计算与良好理论保障的量化方法。

Method: 提出一种加抖动的哈达玛变换量化方案：对输入向量应用单个随机哈达玛变换，再减去一个随机标量偏移，最后进行标量量化。该设计通过引入额外随机性，在几乎不增加计算成本的前提下提升了量化质量。

Result: 证明了该方法是无偏的，并且其均方误差渐近逼近使用真正随机旋转所能达到的最佳性能；具体地，当每坐标使用b比特时，误差为(π√3/2 + o(1))·4⁻ᵇ，其中o(1)项随量化级数增长在所有单位向量和维度下一致趋于零。

Conclusion: 所提出的加抖动哈达玛量化方法在保持O(d log d)低计算复杂度的同时，实现了接近理想随机旋转的量化性能，具有坚实的理论基础和广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Vector quantization via random projection followed by scalar quantization is a fundamental primitive in machine learning, with applications ranging from similarity search to federated learning and KV cache compression. While dense random rotations yield clean theoretical guarantees, they require $Θ(d^2)$ time. The randomized Hadamard transform $HD$ reduces this cost to $O(d \log d)$, but its discrete structure complicates analysis and leads to weaker or purely empirical compression guarantees.
  In this work, we study a variant of this approach: dithered quantization with a single randomized Hadamard transform. Specifically, the quantizer applies $HD$ to the input vector and subtracts a random scalar offset before quantizing, injecting additional randomness at negligible cost. We prove that this approach is unbiased and provides mean squared error bounds that asymptotically match those achievable with truly random rotation matrices. In particular, we prove that a dithered version of TurboQuant achieves mean squared error $\bigl(π\sqrt{3}/2 + o(1)\bigr) \cdot 4^{-b}$ at $b$ bits per coordinate, where the $o(1)$ term vanishes uniformly over all unit vectors and all dimensions as the number of quantization levels grows.

</details>


### [321] [Uncertainty-Driven Anomaly Detection for Psychotic Relapse Using Smartwatches: Forecasting and Multi-Task Learning Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13816)
*Nikolaos Tsalkitzis,Panagiotis P. Filntisis,Petros Maragos,Niki Efthymiou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出两种基于智能手表的框架，用于每日精神病复发的早期检测。第一种预测心脏动态并标记预测与观测特征之间的偏差作为异常指标；第二种采用多任务学习融合睡眠、运动和心脏信号，学习时间感知嵌入并预测测量时间。两者均使用Transformer编码器，通过集成多层感知机估计预测不确定性，生成每日异常分数。尽管各自表现良好，但它们捕捉到互补的生理特征，因此提出晚期融合策略，将两个架构的异常信号整合为统一决策分数。在2023年e-Prevention Grand Challenge数据集上，融合模型相比基线实现8%的相对提升，验证了多种数字表型（心脏、运动、睡眠）融合对高保真复发检测的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在真实世界可穿戴设备中面临数据变异性和生理信号复杂性挑战，难以有效识别精神病复发的早期迹象。需要一种鲁棒且能整合多源生理数据的连续被动监测框架，以提升复发检测的准确性和可靠性。

Method: 开发两种基于Transformer的智能手表信号处理框架：一是基于心脏动态预测的异常检测；二是融合睡眠、运动和心脏信号的多任务学习框架，通过时间感知嵌入与测量时间预测增强建模能力。采用集成多层感知机估计预测不确定性，生成每日异常分数，并通过晚融合策略整合两者的异常信号。

Result: 在2023年e-Prevention Grand Challenge数据集上，所提融合模型相较比赛获胜基线实现8%的相对性能提升。消融实验表明，各信号模态贡献显著，多源信息融合优于单一模态，验证了方法在真实场景下的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 整合心脏、运动与睡眠等多源数字表型，结合深度学习与不确定性建模，是实现高精度、高保真精神分裂症复发早期检测的关键。晚融合策略有效利用互补特征，显著提升实际应用中的检测性能。

Abstract: Digital phenotyping enables continuous passive monitoring of behavior and physiology, offering a promising paradigm for early detection of psychotic relapse. In this work, we develop and systematically study two smartwatch-based frameworks for daily relapse detection. The first forecasts cardiac dynamics and flags deviations between predicted and observed features as indicators of abnormality. The second adopts a multi-task formulation that fuses sleep with motion and cardiac-derived signals, learning time-aware embeddings and predicting measurement timing. Both pipelines use Transformer encoders and output a daily anomaly score, derived from predictive uncertainty estimated via an ensemble of multilayer perceptrons to improve robustness to real-world wearable variability. While each framework independently demonstrates strong predictive power, we show that they capture complementary physiological signatures. Consequently, we propose a late-fusion strategy that synergistically combines the anomaly signals from both architectures into a unified decision score. We benchmark our methodology on the 2nd e-Prevention Grand Challenge dataset, where our fused model achieves a 8% relative improvement over the competition-winning baseline. Our results, supported by extensive ablation studies, suggest that the integration of diverse digital phenotypes, cardiac, motion, and sleep, is essential for the high-fidelity detection of psychotic relapse in real-world settings.

</details>


### [322] [Topology-Preserving Neural Operator Learning via Hodge Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13834)
*Dongzhe Zheng,Tao Zhong,Christine Allen-Blanchette*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从函数空间视角研究了在几何网格上物理场方程的解算子，揭示了霍奇正交性通过隔离不可学习的拓扑自由度与可学习的几何动力学，从根本上解决了谱干扰问题，实现了局限于保持结构子空间的加法逼近。基于霍奇理论和算子分裂，推导出一种原则性的算子级分解方法，提出一种混合欧拉-拉格朗日架构，引入称为霍奇谱对偶性（HSD）的代数级归纳偏置。利用离散微分形式捕捉主导拓扑成分，通过正交辅助环境空间表示复杂局部动力学。该方法在几何图上实现了更高的精度与效率，并更好地保持物理守恒量。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理几何网格上的物理场方程时，难以有效区分拓扑与几何动态，导致谱干扰和物理不变量失真。需要一种能从函数空间角度系统分离拓扑与几何成分的方法，以提升模型的准确性与物理一致性。

Method: 基于霍奇理论与算子分裂，构建了一种算子级分解框架，采用离散微分形式表示拓扑主导部分，引入正交辅助空间表示局部动态，形成具有霍奇谱对偶性（HSD）的混合欧拉-拉格朗日架构。

Result: 所提方法在几何图上显著提升了求解精度与计算效率，同时更准确地保持了物理守恒律，如能量、动量等，验证了其在物理信息建模中的优越性。

Conclusion: 霍奇谱对偶性为物理场建模提供了新的函数空间视角，通过结构保持的分解方式，实现对拓扑与几何动态的精准分离，是提升科学机器学习模型物理一致性和泛化能力的关键。

Abstract: In this paper, we study solution operators of physical field equations on geometric meshes from a function-space perspective. We reveal that Hodge orthogonality fundamentally resolves spectral interference by isolating unlearnable topological degrees of freedom from learnable geometric dynamics, enabling an additive approximation confined to structure-preserving subspaces. Building on Hodge theory and operator splitting, we derive a principled operator-level decomposition. The result is a Hybrid Eulerian-Lagrangian architecture with an algebraic-level inductive bias we call Hodge Spectral Duality (HSD). In our framework, we use discrete differential forms to capture topology-dominated components and an orthogonal auxiliary ambient space to represent complex local dynamics. Our method achieves superior accuracy and efficiency on geometric graphs with enhanced fidelity to physical invariants. Our code is available at https://github.com/ContinuumCoder/Hodge-Spectral-Duality

</details>
